Central Propaganda Department Hosts the Press 66

Shao Yuanchong Reports on Party History Work The Central Propaganda Department held a press conference in the Central Second Conference Room at 2:00 p.m. on the 3rd. More than 20 reporters from various newspapers attended. Zhang Tingxiu presided and read the will of Sun Yat-sen, followed by a report by Central Committee member Shao Yuanchong, who stated that the Central Committee had been preparing for a long time for the Party History work. Due to the busy schedule of Party affairs, the Party History and Historical Materials Compilation Committee was established at the end of April this year. Its significance is that every country or social group must have a corresponding history after a considerable period of time. In particular, political parties, labor groups, and social groups in Europe and the United States all have a detailed history after a certain number of years. Based on this, the importance of historical significance is extremely evident. Our party has struggled for decades and has had a significant impact on the country and the people. To date, there is no concrete Party history for the people to understand, which has led to erroneous or deliberately fabricated facts in recent publications about Party history, causing errors in the thinking of young people. The Central Committee, in light of this, established this committee. The first step is to collect, organize, and review the work. Eleven members are recommended by the Central Committee to be responsible for organizing this committee. These eleven members have a long history with the party and are extremely loyal. Among these eleven members, five standing committee members are also recommended. The committee has more than 30 compilers who are divided into specialized compilers and honorary compilers. They are responsible for compiling and collecting materials. In terms of administrative affairs, a secretariat has been formed. In addition, there are two sections for collection and compilation, as well as a historical materials and archives section and a historical materials exhibition room. Currently, the internal organization, except for the exhibition room, is completely organized. As for the work, it is divided into five groups. The first is the Biography Editing Group of Sun Yat-sen, which plans to compile a long biography first. The current focus is on several points: (1) Sun Yat-sen's speeches, actions, and revolutionary program, (2) all the Party's propositions and movements, (3) the general social history of China, (4) the facts of international aggression against China in recent decades. The second is the Party Yearbook Editing Group, the third is the Collection Group, the fourth is the Organization Group, and the fifth is the Review Group. In addition, the work is divided into four types: the work of each compiler at one time, the work of two events, the work of three people, and the work of four places. At the same time, the chronology of Sun Yat-sen is actively completed, and external publications about Party affairs are reviewed. Any errors are corrected. This is a glimpse of the work of the committee since its establishment, and it is presented to everyone for their information. After the report, the meeting adjourned.

The Course of Constructing the Port of Huludao 67

The groundbreaking ceremony for the opening of Huludao Port was held on the 2nd. As reported in yesterday's important telegrams, domestic and international opinion circles have repeatedly discussed the issue of opening this port. This reporter specially investigated the original case with the Ministry of Railways and learned a general overview, which is recorded for reference by those who care about current affairs. Huludao is located at the southwestern end of Jin County in Liaoning Province, on the northwest coast of the Bohai Bay, more than seven miles southeast of the Beining Railway, between Yingkou and Qinhuangdao, occupying an important position economically and militarily. During the Qing Dynasty, when Xu Shichang was the Governor-General of the Three Eastern Provinces, he saw that Dalian Bay was thriving under Japanese management and Yingkou was becoming increasingly sluggish. Therefore, he planned to open an ice-free port along the coast of Fengtian Province. In the summer of the 34th year of Guangxu (1908), he hired British engineer Hughes to survey the area, and Huludao was found to be the most suitable. The plan was adopted by the Qing authorities at that time, and in the second year of Xuantong (1910), the project began with the laying of seven miles of railway tracks between Lianshan and Huludao, and the construction of breakwaters. However, the project was suspended after only one year of construction due to the outbreak of the revolution and the lack of funds. After the establishment of the Republic of China, some construction work was carried out, but from the second to the fourth year of the Republic of China (1913-1915), the road and port business made no progress. In the fifth year of the Republic of China (1916), Chen Yingnan, the general manager of the Tongsu Railway Company, sought to export coal from Jinxi and petitioned the authorities for a port construction plan. By the eighth year of the Republic of China (1919), the European War had ended, and British and American capitalists paid attention to the East Asian issue, and suggested to our country's authorities to build Huludao Seaport and lay the Jin'ai Railway (that is, with Huludao as the starting point). The authorities of the Eastern Provinces then had the plan to build Huludao Port, and the long-standing pending case was therefore brought up again. At the same time, the Ministry of Communications in Beijing also had this proposal. As a result, the Eastern Provinces and the Ministry of Communications jointly organized the project, and the funding was set at 10 million yuan. The Ministry of Communications obtained British understanding and withdrew 5 million yuan from the interests of the Jingfeng Railway, and concluded five outline articles, appointing Zhou Zhaoxiang as the director of the port opening. Later, the project was suspended again due to frequent wars. In the eleventh year of the Republic of China (1922), the Zhili-Fengtian War broke out, and the agreement between the Ministry of Communications and the Eastern Provinces to build the port was cancelled. The Eastern Provinces then operated it independently, but it was interrupted due to financial difficulties. Until the autumn of last year (the 18th year of the Republic of China, 1929), when Sun Zhesheng, the Minister of Railways, inspected the Beining, Banhan, PingSui, and other roads, he went to Shenyang to discuss with Zhang Xueliang, the authority of the Northeast. After the Beining Railway was unified and managed by the Ministry, he also considered that the Huludao port opening policy was included in the Premier's industrial plan, which was very important for the development of the Beining Road's business and the Northeast's foreign transportation. Therefore, it was agreed that 500,000 yuan would be retained monthly from the Beining Road's business surplus as a special fund for operating the Huludao project. In January of the 19th year of the Republic of China (1930), Gao Jiyi, the director of the Beining Railway Bureau, and the representative of the Dutch Port Management Company in China signed a contract in Tianjin to build the Huludao Seaport, with a funding of 6.4 million US dollars. The main points of this construction project are as follows: (1) The south section of the breakwater is 4,100 feet long, and the southwest section is 1,000 feet long. (2) The total length of the wharf wall in the port is 3,700 feet. (3) The working wharf is 900 feet long. (4) The guide dike, north of the working wharf in the port, is 2,360 feet long, and the one west of Banlashan is 2,500 feet long. (5) A part of the waterway in the port is dredged to 27 feet below zero, and a part to 32 feet below zero. The port gate waterway is dredged to 30 feet below zero, with a bottom width of 650 feet and a length of about 1,500 feet, to a depth of 30 feet below zero at the seabed. (6) The Dagwa and the near-sea areas, and the area between the breakwater and the wharf wall, are filled to 22 feet above zero. (7) Banlashan and Gaoliangtou Dui, these two mountains are leveled to 22 feet above zero. According to the contract, all projects are scheduled to be completed before October 15th of the 24th year of the Republic of China (1935). At the same time, a port affairs office is specially set up under the Beining Railway Bureau to manage the port affairs projects of Huludao and Yingkou, which are affiliated to the road. Lin Yimin is appointed by the Ministry of Railways as the director and chief engineer of the office, and Ning Wu is the deputy director. The office has two sections, affairs and engineering, and several engineers to take charge of the project. This project has started in May of this year and is scheduled to hold a groundbreaking ceremony on July 2nd. Minister Sun of the Ministry of Railways invited Wu Tiecheng to participate in the ceremony as a representative. Thus, the long-cherished wish of many years has been realized again. The Three Eastern Provinces have long been in the hands of Japan and Russia. In recent years, the railways built by themselves, such as the Shenhai, Jihai, Qike, Datong, and Taosuo lines, as well as the Beining Line, the only trunk line in the Northeast, have all become the cultivation lines of the Zhongdong and Manchu Railways. In particular, the Manchu Railway receives the benefits of our railways. In the future, after the completion of Huludao, the dependence on others in the past can be replaced by having our own seaport to swallow goods. It is truly of great significance to the prosperity of transportation in the Northeast and the national economy and people's livelihood.

The Fujian Navy and Army Jointly Attack Lu's Troops 68

Liu Heding advances from eastern Fujian.

Fang Shengtang advances from southern Fujian.

Lu Xingrong defends alone.

Lin Zhong resigns from all concurrent positions.

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since the National Government explicitly ordered that the navy and army under Lu's command in Fujian plan to advance, it is now found that this general attack is divided into two routes. The eastern Fujian route is under the responsibility of Liu Heding, who will take Gutian and Yanping from Minqing and Yongtai, and the arrangements have been completed. The military supplies and salaries supplied by the headquarters have also been transported, and they can advance as soon as the order is given. The southern Fujian route is under the responsibility of Fang Shengtang. After arriving in Xiamen, Fang immediately convened representatives Zhang Zhen, Xiao Shuxuan, and Chen Guohui (Chen's arrest warrant has now been revoked by the National Government) to hold a military meeting. It was decided that all of Xiao and Chen's troops would be dispatched, and Fang would personally take command. Zhang would be responsible for the rear supply, and would also send troops to assist when necessary. In order to facilitate military operations, the two troops were reorganized into wartime formations, with each troop reorganized into two detachments, with each detachment consisting of two battalions. Once the provincial government launches the attack, Chen's troops will enter Youxi from Dehua, and Xiao's troops will enter Datian from Anxi at the same time, so that Lu's troops will be attacked from both sides. It is planned that the eastern Fujian route will first attack Yanping, and the southern Fujian route will first attack Youxi, in order to break Lu's base. The rest will be easy to solve. As for the Haiyan aircraft, it has arrived in Fujian for many days. According to visitors to the pilot of this aircraft, after the aircraft arrived on the 15th, it went to the front line on the 16th to distribute leaflets, and on the 17th, it carried four bombs to attack the enemy's position. On the morning of the 18th, it drove to Baisha and looked down at the enemy troops gathered in the temple below, and bombed the temple with bombs, killing many enemies. At the same time, it felt thick smoke rushing upwards in the air, presumably the enemy was shooting with rifles, but the rifles could only reach 2,000 meters, and the aircraft was flying between 3,500 meters and 4,000 meters, so how could it hit? On the 19th, it went to inspect the upper reaches of Baisha and found four steamships and sparrow boats with the flag of Lu Xinming's headquarters hanging on them. It quickly dropped a bomb on one of them, and the rest scattered. On the 20th, it went to scout and found that the enemy had retreated. On the 11th, it went to Baisha again and found no trace of the enemy. It is also said that there are three aircraft transported to Fujian this time. In addition to the Haiyan, which has already flown, the rest are being assembled at the Mawei Aircraft Factory. The horsepower and speed are better than the Haiyan.

As for Lu's troops, Lu Xingming did not agree with the detention of the members of the provincial government, so he went elsewhere beforehand. Lu Xingbang did not agree to start a war with Liu Heding's division, and has returned to Youxi after the war. Now all the military affairs of Lu's side are presided over by Lu Xingrong alone. Lu believes that the failure of this attack on the provincial capital was also due to the poor quality of the military equipment. For example, the barrel of a rifle would be burst by the heat after firing, making it unusable. Even the bullets would sometimes misfire and fly backwards out of the barrel. The cannons could not bloom or aim accurately, and only a hollow sound was heard, and the shells drilled into the soil intact. It is found that most of these guns and bullets were manufactured by Chen Zhongcong, the chief of the staff, when he was the director of the Huangdian Arsenal. At that time, more than one million yuan was spent, but only such products were produced. Therefore, Lu's troops were angry and took the Yanping factory technician Li and the Youxi factory supervisor Zheng to Youxi for investigation. At the same time, because there were many casualties in this war, rebellious soldiers and bandits were specially recruited to supplement the troops. The recruits who have been recruited include Chen Guocun's rebellious regiment in Shuikou, Zhou Zhiqun's rebellious brigade in Yanping, and about 1,000 bandits from Wu Da'ang and Huang Qilan, who are guarding Yongtai. They are still in a stalemate with the Lishui police team under Liang Jichuan. Xu Feilong and Fei Feng's two groups of more than 1,000 people are guarding Dehua, and are currently fighting with Zhang Zhen's division and Lin Qinglong's regiment. As for Gutian, it is guarded by Chen Rongbiao's regiment, and Youxi is guarded by Ye Xingxin's regiment. Behind them, the defenses of Shaowu and Jian'ou are under the responsibility of Huang Qingcai and Cheng Bingyao's regiments. Therefore, these two regiments are both from Minqing, and Lu Xingrong does not trust them very much. Lin Zhong, the brigade commander of the 1st Marine Brigade and the commander of the provincial defense, was also one of those who advocated the detention of the members of the provincial government and the provincial party department during the January 6th coup in the provincial capital. This war has not shown any signs of maintaining local security. However, he suddenly submitted his resignation to the Marine Corps Command and the provincial government, resigning from his positions as brigade commander of the 1st Brigade and commander of the provincial defense. It has been approved, and the provincial defense headquarters has been explicitly abolished by the provincial government. The headquarters of the 1st Brigade is planning to transfer Jin Zhenzhong, the regiment commander of the 1st Regiment of the brigade, to be promoted to the position, and Lin will be transferred to be a senior advisor to the headquarters. (June 27th)

Reorganization of the Wuhan Municipal Government 70

Ordered that the words "Special Municipality" be removed from all bureaus.

Report to the Executive Yuan and inform the citizens.

Hankou Correspondence: Since the Hankou Special Municipal Government received the order from the National Government that the special municipalities of Nanjing, Shanghai, Beiping, Qingdao, Tianjin, and Guangzhou should all be renamed, it immediately prepared for reorganization in accordance with the new organization law and decided to implement it on July 1st. Today (July 1st), the municipal government and its subordinate bureaus have all been renamed, and Mayor Liu Wendao has reported the reorganization to the Executive Yuan for record and informed the citizens. The proclamation reads: "It is found that the National Government Gazette No. 501 contains the order of the National Government on June 20th, which states that the special municipalities of Nanjing, Shanghai, Hankou, Beiping, Qingdao, Tianjin, and Guangzhou are renamed as cities, and all previous appointments of mayors of the special municipalities should be revoked in accordance with the newly formulated organization law and reappointed. This order also received the National Government's appointment certificate, appointing Liu Wendao as the mayor of Hankou City. This order, etc., is hereby ordered to be followed. The name of this special municipality is changed to Hankou City on July 1st, and the name of the Hankou Special Municipal Government is changed to the Hankou Municipal Government. All subordinate bureaus, offices, and associations shall remove the word "Special" from their names on the same day. However, Article 2 of the newly promulgated organization law stipulates that a city may be established under the direct jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan if the place where people live has one of the following conditions: 1. The capital; 2. A population of more than one million; 3. A special political and economic situation, etc. Hankou meets the provisions of Article 2 of the new organization law and should be renamed Hankou City under the direct jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan, and has been ordered by the Executive Yuan to the same effect as before. However, before the new seal is received, this government and all bureaus will temporarily borrow the old seal. In addition to reporting to the Executive Yuan for record and issuing separate orders, this proclamation is hereby issued to inform all citizens." Guangdong, Hong Kong, and Macau.

General Shareholder Vote of the Steamboat Company 71

Ho Tung elected as chairman of the board.

Hong Kong Correspondence: The Guangdong-Hong Kong-Macau Steamboat Company, which travels between Guangzhou, Hong Kong, and Macau, convened a general shareholder vote on June 24 to decide on Ho Tung's proposal to "take back the Chinese cargo and passenger business for the company to operate on its own or to transfer it to new contractors." It is found that the origin of the voting meeting was that the company held an extraordinary shareholders' meeting on March 4, and the majority approved Ho's proposal. However, the chairman of the company believed that many shareholders from afar were not present to vote and did not approve the passage, and it was necessary to convene a formal vote of all shareholders or representatives to resolve the issue. Therefore, it was changed to June 24. On the day of the vote, the voting inspectors Guan Yaoguang were selected by Ho's side first, and the voting inspector Blaton was selected by the other side to inspect the number of shares, the number of votes, and supervise everything. The voting started at 11 o'clock. The total number of shares in the company was 80,000 shares. Except for 3,447 shares that were transferred after March 4 and lost their voting rights according to the rules, the number of shares with voting rights on that day was actually 76,553 shares. The Western shareholders who attended the voting were Maiqi Xia Weishi Hualun Luoda, etc., and the Chinese shareholders were He Dong Li Zifang Luo Wenjin Liu Yulin, etc. At 4 o'clock in the afternoon, Chairman Maiqi arrived and announced the end of the voting. The voting results were calculated on the spot. The number of votes for Ho Tung's side was 53,082 shares, or 6,387 votes, the number of votes for the other side was 8,945 shares, or 1,319 votes, and the number of neutral votes was 13,026 shares, or 1,859 votes. According to the statistics, the number of votes for Ho Tung was 44,137 shares more than the other side, or 5,068 votes. Ho Tung's proposal was officially passed. In addition, the directors of the company held a board meeting in the conference room on the 25th and immediately elected Ho Tung as the new chairman of the board. After this case was decided, all the Chinese cargo and passenger business was taken back by the company for its own operation, and the board of directors entrusted Ho with full power to handle it. Attached is Ho Tung's proposal to the shareholders on December 2, 1929, as follows: (A) It is about the renewal of the contract between the company's ships and the Chinese passengers and cargo and the former contractor, but because the contractor competes with the company for business, it is detrimental to the company's interests. (B) The shareholders hereby notify the board of directors to cancel this method and formulate a new method to give priority to those who do not compete with the company and give them a new contract or take back the company's own operation.

Suspicion Issues of the Xu Zhuoran Case 72

Jimei schools help Ye Yuan.

Xiamen Correspondence on the 30th: The case of Xu Zhuoran's assassination has been ordered by the National Government to be thoroughly investigated and arrested by the Fujian Provincial Government and the Zhangxia Naval Police. In Fujian Province, it is a rare and serious case. When Xu was assassinated, Chen Yanxiang, the director of Jimei School and the manager of Tong'an Tongmei Automobile Company, was detained by the police at the request of Xu's family on suspicion and sent to the court for investigation. Xu accompanied Chen Yanxiang from Tong'an to Jimei School to visit Ye Yuan on the evening of the 27th, and stayed at the school that night to discuss important matters in Xiamen the next day. At about 5:00 a.m. on the 28th, he accompanied Chen to Antai Heshuitou. Ye first went to Xiamen and left a name card at the Jimei Station with the words "Telephone No. 870, Fengyi Qianzhuang, Taishi Lane." Xu and Chen arrived in Xiamen at 1:00 p.m. and came to Fengyi with Chen, and Xu was assassinated outside the door in front of Fengyi. Xu's family believes that outsiders do not know about the meeting between Xu and Ye in Xiamen. Ye's name card has an address but no reason, and there is no name of Xu Zhuoran who received the name card. The meeting between Xu and Ye in Fengyi is only a tacit agreement and is not known to outsiders. It is believed that Ye has a suspicion of arranging a murder in advance. As for Chen Yanxiang, it is believed that he deliberately delayed the time at the Meirengong Station for more than ten minutes, and Xu waited downstairs before accompanying Xu to Fengyi. When he arrived at the Hengsheng Street intersection, he asked to lead the way forward for nearly ten steps, and Xu was assassinated outside the door after Chen entered the Fengyi gate. It is believed that Chen deliberately delayed the time at the station so that the front of the Fengyi gate could be arranged calmly, and that the lead should be parallel and should not go forward for nearly ten steps, deliberately avoiding the danger of conspiring to assassinate. After Ye was arrested, all the teachers and staff of Jimei requested bail, and the students also sent representatives to request bail, but the court refused. Teachers and staff, such as teachers and directors, resigned, and students went on strike to help Ye. School Principal Chen Jiageng repeatedly telegraphed the headquarters, the court, and Xu's funeral office to ease Ye's situation. Ye also issued a statement stating that he was separated from Jimei School because of the Xu case, and stated that he and Xu were close friends. This time, Xu came to discuss the fundraising for the teaching group and had to go to Xiamen to discuss the joint lease of the Tongmei car road with the Anxi Automobile Company. He did not know when Xu would come on the morning of the 28th. If something had to be done first, leaving a name card was to show the address so that he could call to contact him. There is no such thing as arranging a murder. As for Chen Delin, who was captured by the teaching group in Tong'an, he claimed that Ye Yuan and Chen Yanxiang were the masterminds, and that he was entrusted by Ye to find assassins. As a result, he found three people. When Xu was assassinated, he was on the scene to supervise the plan, which was all made by Ye and Chen. After Chen Delin confessed, the Siming District Court of Xiamen entrusted the Tong'an Judicial Office to review the confession. The confession was the same as before, and the confession was very long. The Zhangxia Police Headquarters twice increased the reward to 2,000 yuan for arresting the murderer in the Xu case. After Chen Delin confessed the names and addresses of the three murderers, Lin Ming, the captain of the detective team of Siming County, Xiamen, led all the detectives and 16 members of the Public Security Bureau's Browning team to capture Lin Luo, one of the shooters, in Neilin Township, Tong'an, on the morning of the 22nd, and escorted him to the headquarters. After two interrogations by the military law office and one court interrogation, the secret confession was made. The Jimei School and Tong'an schools jointly organized a Ye Aid Committee and issued a declaration to defend Ye, saying that Chen Delin had a grudge against Ye and falsely accused him, and that Delin had a good impression of Xu Zhuoran. Ye had no reason to use Chen to kill Xu. However, on the 27th, Xu's funeral office issued a telegram from Xu Zhuoran's wife, also strongly pointing out that Ye and Chen committed a major suspicion of murder, and urged the authorities to speed up the execution. On the 29th, Ye also issued a letter to School Principal Chen Jiageng, saying, "Chen Delin falsely accused me of conspiring with Yanxiang three weeks before the assassination of Xu, telling me in the Science Museum (Jimei School) that he wanted to deal with Xu and wanted to find a brave person. Lin Luo was introduced by him, and then Lin Ke and Lin Yuan were introduced by Lin Luo. Yanxiang had disagreements with the recent reasons for the civil nine turmoil and the Tong'an Education Association elections. As for Xu, he recently relied on Xu to argue with Regiment Commander Xiao to get his job back when he was investigated by the army because of the Tongmei car road. Chen Fangde Xu was too busy, how could he conspire with me to kill Xu? Delin is closer to Xu than to me, and has a deep grudge against me. How can he conspire with me to kill Xu? Pan Tu (affiliated to the inland) is a place of evil, stealing my cattle and wood from the agricultural and forestry school. I have filed a case in Tong'an, how can I ask Tu Pan to kill the reason why the four parties can never work together and falsely accuse them of conspiring to assassinate? How can there be such a thing in the world? Also, Delin confessed that the reason why I killed Xu was because Xu destroyed my Tong'an Anxi liaison plan. I have been concentrating on Jimei school affairs for ten years as one day. I have never heard of any party, government, or military matters. What is the so-called Anxi Tong'an liaison plan?" This case is still under investigation by all parties, and all parties are paying close attention to it.

Mo Runxun, the director of the Public Security Bureau of Jiaxing County, last month, because the army was dispatched to hire corvée, the majority of the farmers in the Tanghui Town were affected. Kunshan 74

Three organizations establish a parity bureau: In recent days, the rice price in Kunyi has been high, and each stone of white winter has risen to 21 yuan, and the stock of rice in each rice shop is still scarce, and there is a trend of rising. The patrol leader and police officer abducted women: Wang Jinlin, who opened a tofu shop on the north bank of the city, has a daughter named Xiuying, who is only seventeen years old and has a slight appearance. Also, Gu, the wife of Gu Zhuxue, who collects pig intestines in the same place, and Pan Fuchang, a police officer, have been having an affair for more than a day. Suzhou 76

Investigation of Prisoners Detained in Military Prison: President Lin of the Higher Court, based on telegrams from the Shanghai and Wu County Lawyers' Associations stating that thirty first-class defendants transferred to the Army Prison were unable to endure the harsh treatment of the military prison, requested their immediate return for detention and minor punishment, as well as the dismissal of the three section chiefs, including Ding Lei. Yesterday, he specially appointed Yao Guozhang, the prison section chief, to go to the military prison for investigation to clarify the truth. After receiving the commission, Chief Yao went to the military prison for a detailed investigation of everything and immediately returned to the court to report. According to him, the first-class defendants had not had their hair shaved, nor had they suffered from cold or hunger. However, the management was stricter according to military prison rules. There were matters of shackles and fetters; shackles were used, but not fetters. As for food, it was more abundant than in ordinary prisons, with an increase of three cents per person, totaling fifteen cents. Family visits were allowed only once a month.

Impersonating Wounded Soldiers and Parading in the Streets: After the establishment of the Joint Military-Police Inspection Office, on the afternoon of the day before yesterday (2nd), hooligans such as Ding Lao San and others impersonated wounded soldiers to incite rumors. They were caught by the patrol team of the Inspection Office and taken in for questioning. They confessed to impersonating wounded soldiers without denial. Yesterday (3rd), the office specially ordered the team to suppress Ding Lao San and parade him in the streets as a warning.

Prohibition of Iron Shops Casting Weapons: The Military-Police Inspection Office decided at yesterday's meeting to prohibit blacksmith shops from casting weapons. If anyone is found privately casting such items, they will be severely punished.

Seven Prisoners Granted Parole: Xie Fuci, warden of the Third Jiangsu Prison in Xiaoliu Zhen Lane, believed that seven prisoners, including Li Xin You, had consistently shown good behavior and genuine repentance. He specially petitioned the Higher Court Procuratorate to forward the request to the Ministry of Justice for approval of their parole. The parole ceremony was scheduled for 2:00 PM on the 5th of this month. The names, ages, and crimes of the seven prisoners are summarized below: (1) Li Xin You, 45 years old, Anhui native, robbery, originally sentenced to life imprisonment; (2) Chen A Gen, 42 years old, Changshu native, robbery, life imprisonment; (3) Xu Shao Lun, 32 years old, Ningbo native, murder, first-class imprisonment of 12 years; (4) Qian A Xiao, 35 years old, Wu County native, robbery, first-class 10 years; (5) Chen Qi Da, 46 years old, Wu County native, robbery, second-class 8 years; (6) Jiang Zhao Ji, 36 years old, Wu County native, robbery, first-class 10 years; (7) Ma Xi Jin, 37 years old, Wu County native, robbery, originally sentenced to 7 years.

Wuxi 78

Deputy Township Chief Arrested for Smoking: Wu Jiangbo, deputy chief of the Second District (Jingyun City) of Wujiang Township, and Wu Zude, deputy chief of Xiang township, were deeply addicted and their behavior was corrupt, causing considerable dissatisfaction among the villagers. At 3:30 PM on the day before yesterday, Wu Zude went to a certain opium den in Nanmen Yaoshang to smoke. Chen, the police chief of the Second Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau, led police officers to investigate and arrest him on the spot. Wu Zude, Wang Er, Qiu Apan, and three others, along with smoking paraphernalia, were taken to the bureau. Chief Zhu of the sub-bureau held a preliminary hearing, and all three confessed to smoking opium. They were immediately prepared for transfer to the Public Security Bureau for transfer to the County Government for interrogation. Bizarre Murder Case: Suspect Arrested: Wen Da, grandson of Qiang Tingzhi, a resident of Figure 573, Qiangjiaqiao, Meicun Town, Beixia Township, of the county, was eight years old and attending a nearby primary school. He did not return after school at 5:00 PM on the 20th of last month and could not be found. On the 30th, Wen Da's body was found in a river near Meicun. His skin color had changed and his condition was miserable. Qiang Tingzhi ordered someone to retrieve the body and place it on the shore, while investigating the cause of Wen Da's death. It was discovered that Cha Xiangchu, a nearby villager, was suspected of kidnapping. However, Cha had already gone to the city the next day and stayed at the Mengyuan Inn on the road. Qiang immediately tracked him down the next morning, found Cha, and dragged him to the Second Sub-Bureau of Public Security, requesting an investigation. Chief Sun of the sub-bureau held a preliminary hearing. Qiang Tingzhi provided the same information as before. Cha Xiangchu claimed that he did not know Wen Da and that Qiang was fabricating accusations. Chief Sun of the sub-bureau, based on the information provided, said that since the matter concerned a murder case, he would wait to transfer the case to the bureau for interrogation. Qiang Tingzhi was ordered to return. At 5:00 PM in the afternoon, Qiang again petitioned the county to send personnel to the countryside for an autopsy. Cheng, the trial officer, held a hearing and then took Shen, the coroner, by boat to the countryside to perform an autopsy in accordance with the law for further processing. Another Smuggling Case: A few days ago, the case of Gu Liuzi, a boatman transporting private soil and Wang, who shipped a large quantity of Yunnan soil from Shanghai, was finally settled. Unexpectedly, the day before yesterday, someone named Jia from Jiangyin, a large soil dealer, brought a large quantity of opium weighing more than 500 taels, worth more than a thousand yuan, to Wuxi and hid near the Gongyun Bridge outside the Guangfu Gate at the Wuxi Hotel. Unexpectedly, the matter was discovered by detectives from a certain agency in the county. Several men in plain clothes went to the hotel to conduct a search, and all the opium, more than 500 taels, was seized. The soil dealer, because the matter violated prohibitions, had no choice but to let them take it and dared not speak out. Detective Chief Shot and Killed in the Capture of Bandits: Recently, there have been kidnapping cases in Yixing County. Sun, the county magistrate of the county, sent police to investigate and discovered that the kidnappings were carried out by bandits from Liao Jiatang in the eastern district of Heqiao in the county. He ordered the police chief to order Detective Chief Qiu Fulin to lead police to encircle and suppress them. Unexpectedly, the bandits opened fire to resist arrest. Qiu bravely took the lead and fought fiercely with the bandits for a long time. As a result, bandits Wang Desheng and Ding, a wealthy man, and seven others were captured. Chief Qiu and police officer Jia Yu Kuan were shot and injured by the bandits. In addition to sending the captured bandits to the county for interrogation, the injured were hired to take a boat to Wuxi for treatment. On the way, Chief Qiu died from his injuries. Jia Yu Kuan was sent to Puren Hospital for treatment, and his injuries were not life-threatening. Inspection of Wounded Soldiers and Armaments: The county government received a secret telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang after 2:00 AM yesterday, stating that some of the wounded soldiers accommodated in rear hospitals had brought firearms with them, which could cause trouble. He ordered a strict inspection. Magistrate Sun immediately met with Commander Chen of the Garrison Regiment in Wuxi, Battalion Commander Jin, and the Public Security Bureau's Police Brigade and went to Huishan at around 5:00 AM to conduct a detailed inspection. Handguns and stray bullets were found on the spot and confiscated. When the inspection was slightly resisted, gunfire resulted, killing one person and injuring four. The situation was extremely serious, but now it has returned to normal. Re-trial of Tan Qixuan Case: After Tan Qixuan, the former director of the Beishang Township Government, was shot and killed by bandits on April 1st of last year, Tan Zhongying, a relative of the deceased, reported to the county and had Lu Shiqiao, a person involved in the case, detained for interrogation. The case has not yet been concluded. The county government issued summons to all persons involved in the case to convene for a joint hearing on the 3rd. However, Lu Fengxiang had already died of illness. Bao Xiaozhai was detained in the third branch of Suzhou Prison for another case and died in prison. Xu Abing had been assassinated. Lu Duanyi was on the run and could not be arrested. Only Yu Yao Cheng and Chen Yan Gong were detained. Tang Yiqin, a member of the case-clearing committee, brought Lu Shiqiao, Bao Dayuan, Lu Genhu, Guo Asi, Zhu Ada, Sun Junxi, and others who were in custody to court for questioning. As a result, Yu Yao Cheng and Chen Yan Gong did not seem to be involved and were released on bail. The others were returned to custody to await the arrival of Tan Qixuan, the plaintiff, and Wang Yinhua and Pu Xiehan, the witnesses, before further interrogation.

In addition, the telephone lines in the city were severely damaged by lightning, and the interior was heavily dampened, causing about 80 to 90 households to have difficulty communicating. A Cigarette Caused Death: Zhou Zimei, the owner of a tofu shop in Zhu Xiangkou, Shaobo Town, in the county, died at 6:00 PM on the 1st at Peide Hospital in the town due to fire poisoning. Because his work was entirely at night, Zhou slept every afternoon. On the day before, Zhou's cigarette ignited the bedding while he was sleeping. The smoke spread slowly. When someone noticed, they called Zhou, who was unaware. He was dragged off the bed from the fire and suddenly awoke. However, his whole body was covered in blisters. He was sent to the hospital for treatment, but because he was deeply poisoned, he eventually died.

Gaoyou 82

Militia Killed Farmer by Mistake While Capturing Bandits: At about 8:00 PM the night before last, seven or eight bandits suddenly came to Zhouxiang Town in the county to rob farmers. A farmer named Liu from the town rushed to the Hudang Village Security Corps to report. The corps immediately sent more than a dozen militiamen to arrest them. When the bandits heard the news, they fled. Liu's eldest and second sons, who were hiding from the bandits in a nearby forest, heard that the bandits had left and went home together. Unexpectedly, the militiamen saw them and mistakenly thought they were bandits and opened fire. The bullet hit Liu's eldest son in the abdomen and he fell to the ground and died.

Pinghu 84

Start of Fair-Price Rice Sales, but Many Still Begging for Rice: The county government, in response to the current rice panic, quickly convened a meeting of various agencies, groups, and representatives from all walks of life to raise funds to handle fair-price rice sales. Fair-price rice sales began on July 1st. The fair-price rice sales locations were divided into the East Bureau and the West Bureau. The East Bureau was located at the Dawang Temple outside the East Gate, and the West Bureau was located at the Yousheng Palace inside the West Gate. In the future, the East and West Bureaus will open on the same day every 1st and 16th of the month from 8:00 AM to 4:00 PM, limiting each household to three sheng at a price of 13 cents per sheng. Yesterday, a large number of rural women, old and young, gathered in the Nanlangxia and outside the East Gate to beg for rice from the various rice shops. The various shops reported to the Public Security Bureau, and Director Wang and Magistrate Fang personally went to persuade the hungry people to go to the bureau to buy rice. The hungry people claimed that they were hungry but had no money.

Price Evaluation Committee Set Rice Prices: The county's rice price evaluation committee met the day before yesterday to set rice prices. It was decided that the price of rice would be 14 yuan and 80 cents per stone, with a maximum of 18 yuan. However, unscrupulous merchants still obeyed in appearance but disobeyed in reality, and the price of each stone rose by another one or two yuan today.

Jiaxing 85

Important Bandits Arrested: The Jiaxing Second District Water Police Division received a report the day before yesterday from a secret agent that several important bandits (subordinates of Ah Shu, a Taibao from Xincang, Pinghu) were hiding in Shengze Town, at the intersection of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Investigation Concluded on Clash Between Militia and Police: A clash occurred between militiamen from the Jiaxing Youchegang Town Local Security Corps and police officers from the town's police substation. He was ordered to pay a cash bail of 100 yuan and released on bail pending prosecution. The others were ordered to leave.

Huzhou 86

Xiao Feng's Shen A'kui Encountered Bandits: Since the national and provincial armies searched and arrested and executed many bandits from the western countryside of Huzhou, it has become increasingly possible to clean up the area. However, sporadic bandits still often rob people on the road in broad daylight. At about 3:00 PM on the 30th of last month, Shen A'kui from Xiaofeng was collecting more than 30 yuan of small pig money near Dipu. While passing through a bamboo forest at the junction of Anxiao, two men wielding iron-wrapped wooden poles in the manner of woodcutters suddenly dragged Shen, tied him to a tree, stuffed his mouth with coarse paper, and searched his body. All of Shen's money, an umbrella, and a silk short shirt were robbed.

Fuxing Village in Wuxing County Begs for Relief: The Fuxing Village Committee in Wuxing County stated that the village's silkworm farming was poor, and most of the villagers were starving. If no measures were taken quickly, it would be difficult to avoid a crisis. It was proposed to hold a porridge kitchen to benefit the poor, but the issue of whether the relief rice could be directly claimed from the relief association was specially petitioned to the county government for instructions. It was heard that the county government had instructed the association after receiving the petition, saying that relief rice should be claimed from the county government, and still wait for the disaster relief association to raise funds before reviewing the case.

Results of Petition from Yarn Industry in Six Counties of Jiaxing: Representatives from the chambers of commerce and sock industries of six counties in Jiaxing, including Shen Shuying, Shen Tingquan, Qian Zupei, Wang Zhongliang, Zhou Yuqing, and Ye Cuian, organized a petition delegation to Hangzhou. It has now been learned that Chairman Wang of the former General Chamber of Commerce accompanied them to the provincial government to meet with Chairman Zhang. Secretary-General Shen received them and detailed the current difficulties and the disparity in yarn donation taxes between Jiangsu and Zhejiang. If the burden were increased again by three to more than thirty times, the industry would inevitably decline. The representatives were directly seeking safety for the yarn industry and indirectly pleading for the poor. Secretary-General Shen, after hearing this, agreed to forward the matter to Chairman Zhang and submit it to the provincial government for discussion. They then went to the Department of Finance to petition. Section Chief Jiang of the Second Section received them and agreed to report to Director Qian for review. The representatives then said goodbye and returned to their residence, where they convened yarn industry representatives who had come to Hangzhou to report on the progress and discuss future measures.

Ningbo 87

Yin County Prisoner Intended to Revolt: Yu A'san, a notorious thief detained in the Yin County District Court detention center, secretly used stones to knock off his shackles at noon on the 29th of last month, and tied them with tape to deceive the guards. Prisoner Wu A'mei also pulled out the nails from his shackles. Yu Shengchuan planned to buy thousands of pounds of bayberries to distribute to the prisoners, using the phrase "eating bayberries" as a signal for a mass revolt. Unexpectedly, the prisoners' plan was not kept secret. When Yu A'san was using stones to knock off his shackles, a guard heard him and reported to Director Liang. That director then confined the prisoners to their cages on the afternoon of the same day and inspected them one by one. He saw that the shackles of the three mentioned above had indeed been broken open, so he nailed on new shackles and reported to President Wang. President Wang went to the center in person for inspection yesterday (1st) and warned the prisoners on the spot not to let similar incidents occur again, otherwise they would be severely punished, and told the staff of the center not to be negligent in their duties and to treat prisoners with both leniency and strictness.

The Municipal Public Fund Property Association is About to Close: The Ningbo Municipal Public Fund Property Management Committee held an emergency meeting on the afternoon of the 1st, chaired by Tu Shixun, and passed a resolution: (1) Approve the municipality's letter stating that since the city does not collect national or provincial taxes, it is unnecessary to continue operating the association. "Resolution" Approve the letter and close down the association. (2) Decide on the date of transfer of the association. "Resolution" Set the date to the 5th of this month and send a letter to the municipality to send personnel to take over and request that funding for May and June be issued in advance to facilitate the closure. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Letter from the Wuxi Medical Association 88

To the Editor: I read a news article in the Wuxi Local Communications column of your newspaper on May 14 entitled "Incompetent Doctor Kills Patient", which stated that Shen Qiqing's son recently contracted a cold and died after being subjected to spinal taps by Dr. Qian Baohua for two consecutive days. This is completely inconsistent with the facts. An investigation revealed that Shen's child fell ill early in the morning on February 7 with symptoms clearly indicative of meningitis. Letters to our association from Western doctors Li Kele and Tan Shumo, who provided follow-up consultations, can prove this. Dr. Qian only treated the child twice on February 7th and 8th. Afterwards, more than 30 Chinese and Western doctors successively provided consultations. He eventually died on May 10 due to an insufficient number of serum injections. This was more than three months after Dr. Qian's initial consultation. The report in your newspaper stated that the death was immediate and had no basis. It also stated that the Shen family would resolve the matter through legal means, which is completely unfounded. In short, the Shen family runs a Chinese medicine business and has always been biased against Western medicine. When their beloved son suddenly contracted severe meningitis and Chinese medicine was ineffective, they reluctantly sought help from Western medicine. Unaware that severe meningitis, after one or two spinal taps and serum injections, would only initially alleviate the condition and that further treatment was still required to eradicate the disease, the family did not heed the advice and turned to Chinese medicine. As a result, the root cause of the disease was not eliminated, it became chronic, and the child became incurable. The family mistakenly blamed Dr. Qian, falsely believing that spinal fluid was the essence of the human body and that removing the essence would prevent the body from recovering. This led to a dispute and the spreading of defamatory rumors to slander him. Our association has dispatched personnel to investigate all aspects of the matter and has clearly held a public meeting for a fair discussion. The results of the discussion have been made into an assessment report, which has been distributed to all sectors of society and published in various local newspapers in our city so that the truth and medical principles can be clarified, eliminating various suspicions and misunderstandings in society and preventing the obstruction of legitimate Western medical treatment in the future. This matter concerns the credibility of the entire Western medical community and the personal reputation of Qian Baohua, and so I have summarized it. I sincerely request that you publish this in the Wuxi Local News column to show fairness and impartiality. The Wuxi Medical Association respectfully submits this on July 1st. Educational News

Important News 89

Ministry of Education Promotes Phonetic Symbols: Committee's Second Discussion Meeting Circumstances: The Ministry of Education is actively promoting phonetic symbols and has sought opinions from various parties to gather ideas. The Ministry of Education's Phonetic Symbol Promotion Committee held its second discussion meeting a few days ago, and all discussions yielded considerable results. The minutes of the second discussion meeting are recorded below. The meeting started at 3:00 PM that afternoon. Attendees were Chiang Menglin, Wu Zhihui, Liu Luyin (representing Fang Zhi), Zhao Yuanren, Zhang Shiyi, Dai Yingguan, Wang Ruichang, Guo Youshou, and Peng Baichuan.

Discussion Items and Results 90

(I) The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association suggests that the Ministry of Education establish a Mandarin Phonetic Symbols Teacher Training Institute. (Discussion Result) Researching Western phonetic symbols and researching Mandarin are two separate matters. Anyone wishing to research Mandarin may be designated by the Ministry to study at several Mandarin schools with proven results in China (such as the Shanghai Foch Road and Hartung Road Mandarin School, etc.). As for requesting the Ministry to establish a Mandarin Phonetic Symbols Teacher Training Institute, the matter is postponed for now. (II) Chuan He and others suggest: 1. Seek to improve the writing system so that phonetic symbols are permanently attached to the side of the character (or above and below the character). (Discussion Result) Already adopted, no further discussion needed. 2. Imitate the "katakana" method of Japanese writing to gradually promote Mandarin phonetic symbols. (Discussion Result) Can be imitated. 3. Notify all printing businesses to modify the typefaces, uniformly adding phonetic symbols to the side of the characters. (Discussion Result) To be handled accordingly. 4. Encourage the newspaper industry to add phonetic symbols to the side of characters within a feasible scope. (Discussion Result) To be handled accordingly. 5. Order subordinate agencies, schools, and organizations to uniformly add phonetic symbols next to the characters when issuing documents to the public in the future. (Discussion Result) To be promoted gradually. 6. Petition the central government to instruct all sectors, including agency names, shop signs, and propaganda slogans, advertisements, etc., to add phonetic symbols to the side of the characters (or above and below the characters). (Discussion Result) To be promoted as soon as possible. 7. When encountering resistance to the promotion, government decrees should be used to assist at any time and place. (Discussion Result) To be handled accordingly. (III) Peng Jianong suggests abolishing the three phonetic symbols 万, 兀, and 广, replacing 万 with 丿 for the rising tone, 兀 with V for the rising tone, and 广 with a space for the departing tone, adding them after each sound. (Discussion Result) Because dialects have five tones, they cannot be replaced. (IV) Lu Zhongyuan suggests that the four tones of characters must be marked when promoting phonetic symbols. (Discussion Result) Agreed. (V) Qiu Yi-wu, Zhou Weiji, and others suggest retaining the entering tone. (Discussion Result) Agreed. (VI) He Shuda suggests that since the national phonetic alphabet has been changed to phonetic symbols, initials, finals, and compound finals should be changed to initial symbols, final symbols, and compound final symbols, and tones should be changed to tone marks. (Discussion Result) Labeling initials, finals, and compound finals can be called initial symbols, final symbols, and compound final symbols. Symbols labeling tones can be called tone marks. Phonetic symbols labeling the national pronunciation can be called standard symbols. Symbols labeling dialectal additions can be called dialectal symbols. (VII) Wang Zuyou submitted phonetic fanqie direct charts. (Discussion Result) Can be used for reference. (VIII) Wang Zuyou suggests: 1. Request the Ministry of Education to instruct all provincial and municipal departments and bureaus to solicit people who are familiar with dialects, have a basic understanding of ancient rhymes, and have a deep understanding of the usage of phonetic symbols to appoint a dialect investigator for each county to create a form and fill in the investigation items one by one. At the same time, the investigator should be appointed as a phonetic symbol guidance specialist, requiring them to report the key points of the guidance results and investigation results to the provincial and municipal departments and bureaus every month, and then the provincial and municipal departments and bureaus will report to the Ministry of Education, which will forward them to the Phonetic Symbol Promotion Committee to collect and compile dialect courses by province. 2. In addition to complying with the order to add instruction in phonetic symbols, each school should also set up a dialect course to identify and annotate each character that can be spoken but cannot be written, so that the spoken and written language can easily converge. As for normal schools, a phonetic course of 360 hours should be required, with half taught in each of the first and second semesters, with a conclusion in the middle. Secondary and vocational schools should receive 180 hours. Senior administrative officials in each province and region should also convene a phonetic symbol training class with a study period of three months. The phonetic course should also be at least 180 hours. Students in each school who fail the phonetic symbol course will not be allowed to advance or be employed (but the phonetic course must also include dialect to broaden its use). 3. The content of the phonetic symbol textbook for civilian literacy should always promote the national pronunciation without abandoning dialects, be suitable for civilian application of common knowledge, and facilitate recitation. 4. Request the Ministry of Education to instruct all provincial and municipal departments and bureaus to instruct their subordinates to set up more phonetic literacy centers and civilian reading rooms (the characters in books and newspapers should uniformly use the national pronunciation on the right and the dialect pronunciation on the left to facilitate the recognition of the national pronunciation from the dialect and then the recognition of characters, that is, official notices should also use this method. 5. Each county education bureau is responsible for setting up more compulsory schools and sending more voluntary teachers, limiting the period from a certain month of this year to a certain month of a certain year as the period for civilian literacy in each county, and those who fail to implement the plan will be dismissed from their posts to show punishment. (Discussion Result) The above suggestions are not without merit and should be carefully considered and adopted separately. New appointee of the Jiangsu Education Department

Three Principles of the People Thousand-Character Textbook Compiled 93

The "Three Principles of the People Thousand-Character Textbook" has now been compiled by the Compilation and Review Department of the Ministry of Education and submitted to the Central Training Department for review before printing. The compilation situation is excerpted below: (1) Before the book was compiled, more than 1,000 commonly used characters were selected from 630,000 characters as the basis for the words used in the book. (2) The book uses precise methods to select the necessary common knowledge of the Three Principles of the People, natural history, geography, hygiene, and other subjects as the material for the textbook. (3) The book is divided into two types, one for children and one for adults, each with 88 lessons divided into four volumes. (4) The book has two purposes: first, to provide people with literacy, and second, to popularize the Three Principles of the People, so the compilation is extremely difficult. In addition, the book was ordered by the Central Government to be compiled by the end of June this year, and the compilation period for the department was only four months. Because the time was short, shortcomings are inevitable, so the current book is designated as a provisional edition. After it is printed and experimented for one year, it is planned to make a thorough revision.

New Plans for Tangshan University 96

Constructing New Dormitories, Increasing Budget

Adding Research Institutes, Improving Curriculum

(Tangshan Correspondence) Since Dr. Li Shutian took office as the president of the Tangshan Civil Engineering College of Jiaotong University in this city on May 10, he has actively rectified all matters within the college, holding successive college affairs meetings and teaching affairs meetings to formulate various plans in order to realize them one by one in the shortest possible time. The following is a summary of the most important ones:

Planning Development Plans: Former President Li Houshen had a draft of the college affairs plan, and all professors jointly drafted a five-year development plan. Professor Chen Maokang also drafted a plan himself. Recently, in order to demonstrate the spirit of cooperation and draw on collective wisdom, all faculty and staff jointly drafted a five-year development plan for the college, which is currently a draft.

Improving the Original Curriculum: In order to meet the needs of the community and seek its own progress, the college has greatly improved the original curriculum and formulated a new curriculum table, which was approved by the Teaching Affairs Meeting and scheduled to be implemented in the 20th year of the Republic of China. As for the 19th year, in consideration of the subjects that students have already learned and have not yet learned, a transitional curriculum table has been formulated for application.

In order to cultivate independent research transportation engineering specialists who are needed for the material construction in the national strategy and to promote transportation technology inventions that are suitable for national conditions and to increase the transportation engineering science needed by the world and mankind, the Institute of Transportation Engineering of Jiaotong University was established in accordance with the organizational outline of Jiaotong University, and twenty articles of the organizational outline were formulated and passed by the College Affairs Meeting. The application has been submitted to the Shanghai General School for review, and it is reported that researchers will be recruited after the summer vacation this year.

Construction of Student Dormitories: In order to increase the opportunity for young people in China to study, the college plans to build four student dormitories in the next few years and plans to build the entire college. The general plan of the college building has been entrusted to the Tianjin Jintai Engineering Company for drawing, and it has been revised and approved by the College Affairs Meeting. The construction will begin after the summer vacation. However, this construction will take at least until the spring of next year to be used, so a temporary dormitory will be built during the summer vacation for application after the start of school after the summer vacation.

Increase in the Annual Budget: The college's current operating expenses are 11,000 yuan per month. Now, due to the planned expansion, in addition to the need to apply for additional funds, the operating expenses have also increased. It is reported that the budget for the 19th year has been drafted and set at 14,000 yuan per month. The increased amount is mostly used for the purchase of books and instruments.

Increase in Sanitary Equipment: In order to increase the health of all faculty and students in the college, the college has requested a certain company in Tianjin to design an increase in the college's sanitary equipment, which is divided into (1) sanitary appliances (2) ditch project (3) tap water project (4) hot water project, totaling about 28,000 yuan. The specifications and plan drawings have been submitted to the Shanghai General School for approval and are expected to be implemented in the near future. Dr. Li Shutian, President of the College, set off for Shanghai on the 21st of this month to discuss various important matters with President Sun Ke. It is expected that there will be a new atmosphere after the start of school after the summer vacation. (Issued on June 26)

Municipal Education Bureau Regulations for Elementary School 98

Graduation Make-Up Examination Method.

August 1st...held separately at Shihua and Shuji.

The first elementary school graduation joint examination held by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has been completed. However, students in various schools who were unable to participate in the joint examination due to illness or special circumstances or whose overall scores were classified as Grade E, resulting in their failure to graduate, are required to be tutored by the schools to make up for their shortcomings. In addition, make-up examination methods are prescribed. The following is a summary: A. Eligibility for Make-Up Examination (1) Those who were unable to participate in the joint examination due to illness or special circumstances and have been approved by the Bureau. (2) Those whose overall scores in the joint examination are classified as Grade E. B. Scope of Make-Up Examination (1) Those who were unable to participate in all or part of the subjects due to illness or special circumstances must make up the subjects in all or part of the subjects. (2) Those whose overall scores in the joint examination are classified as Grade E should make up the subjects in which the students failed. Passing subjects are allowed to be exempted from the examination. C. Method of Score Examination (1) Those who were unable to participate in all subjects due to illness or special circumstances shall be calculated according to the original method of score examination. (2) Those who were unable to participate in some subjects due to illness or special circumstances shall calculate the scores of the subjects to be made up and the scores of the subjects in the joint examination according to the original method of score examination. (3) Those whose overall scores in the joint examination are in Grade E must calculate the scores of each subject after the make-up examination according to the original method of score examination. D. Graduation Standards (1) If the overall score of the make-up examination is calculated according to the score examination method prescribed in item C and is classified as Grade A, B, C, or D, graduation will be granted. (2) Those whose overall score of the make-up examination is still failing will not be allowed to graduate and should repeat the grade. E. Make-Up Examination Date and Time (1) August 1st (2) Arithmetic from 9:00 am to 11:00 am, Party Doctrine from 11:15 am to 11:45 am, Chinese from 1:00 pm to 3:00 pm, Society from 3:15 pm to 3:45 pm, Nature from 4:00 pm to 4:30 pm F. Make-Up Examination Location (1) The make-up examination will be held at the Municipal Shihua Elementary School in Taoshachang, Chengnei: Xicheng, Meixi, Shangwen, Wuben, Chongzheng, Jiangjing, Tangwan, Aiqun, Xiqu, Dyeing Industry, Poor Children's Hospital, Baozha Industry, Linyin, Shihua, Rihua, Yangzheng, Wanzhu, Songxue, Zhengmeng, Zijin, Doumi Industry, Cangji, Chaozong, Jingye, Quanzhang, Mingde Women's Elementary School, Enjing, Chengdong, Yucai, Laixian, Gaochang, Nanqu, Xunyu, Qingxin Affiliated Elementary School, Qingxin Women's Elementary School, Liuyun, Merchant Ship, Puzhong First Affiliated Elementary School, Bide, Tonghui, Dunren, Zhenzhong, Jingcun, Fahua, Honglu, Caonan, Zhoudu, Puzhong Second Affiliated Elementary School (2) The make-up examination will be held at the Municipal Shuji Elementary School in Tianhou Temple: Peiben, Huifeng, Dexin, Yude, Guangzhao Women's Elementary School, Chongsan, Shanggong, Guangzhao Affiliated Elementary School, Zhonghua Affiliated Elementary School, Sanmin, Hubei, Limin, Guangdong Affiliated Elementary School, Xiude, Shanggong Children, Lubin, Shuji, Feihong, Huzhou Shanghai, Minsheng Affiliated Elementary School, Aiguo Affiliated Elementary School, Yongxing, Tanzhen, Pengpu, Sanyu, Suzhou Shanghai, Minzhi, Nanyang Women's Elementary School, Yinxi, Yucai, Peide, Chengzhong Affiliated Elementary School, Zhaoshang Affiliated Elementary School, Zhuzhai, Xijiang, Qiujiang, Dongjiang, Wusong, Peiji, Minguo, Zhenru, Yinxing, Shicun, Ningbo Tongxianghui Elementary School A. Announcement (1) Test paper will be prepared by the Bureau. (2) Each school is responsible for the lunch and transportation of the examinees.

Problem of Recovering Educational Rights in Concessions 100

Municipal Government Asks Construction Committee for Discussion.

The issue of educational rights in the concessions was previously proposed by Chen Dezheng, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, and the Citizens' Federation suggested it to the Municipal Government. However, the Municipal Government considered the matter important and specially asked the Construction Discussion Committee to include it in the agenda to make it perfect. The original letter is excerpted as follows: We have previously received a letter from your committee stating that Commissioner Chen Dezheng proposed to recover the educational rights in the Shanghai concessions. The 9th Standing Committee Meeting of our association has decided to send a letter to the Municipal Government for consideration and handling. The original proposal is enclosed for verification and handling. Upon receiving this, the Municipal Government had already considered this case. Later, it received a letter from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and a proposal from the Education Bureau and the Preparatory Committee of the Citizens' Federation of the Special Zone of this city. After detailed consideration, it was considered that the matter involved foreign affairs and that it was necessary to gather wisdom and conduct practical research to avoid inappropriate measures. It is planned that the Municipal Government will organize a committee to invite prominent figures from all walks of life and Chinese directors of the concessions as consultants, and appoint the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, the Director of the Education Bureau, and the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau as members of the committee to jointly discuss concrete measures and submit them to the Municipal Government for approval before negotiating with the concession authorities to promote the smooth and far-reaching achievement of the recovery of educational rights. However, the previous measures are extremely important and have value for discussion. We should ask your committee to include them in the agenda of the next meeting and submit them for discussion to make them perfect. The original letter is enclosed, along with the letter from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the report and attachments from the Education Bureau and the Preparatory Committee of the Citizens' Federation of the Special Zone of this city. Japanese Expedition 107

Players' Performance at Harbin: Discus and Shot Put Inferior to Russians, Yasushiba's 800 Meters Suppressed by Wang Mingshen. A group of twenty athletes from the Harbin delegation, who are to participate in the International Student Games to be held in Darmstadt on August 7th of this year, arrived at Harbin at 8:00 AM on the 25th. They took a break at the Nagoya Hotel, using it as a resting place. After resting for three hours, they went to the First Sports Field for practice at around 11:00 AM, stopping at 12:40 PM due to the urgency of catching the 3:35 PM Eurasian train. They then left the field and returned to their residences. The audience was enthusiastic. Although it was only a practice session, the scale was no less impressive than previous public sports meetings. Generally, Chinese and foreign sports enthusiasts, feeling the interest in sports, took time out of their busy schedules to watch. By around 10:00 AM, the stands were packed with over two thousand Chinese, Japanese, and Russian spectators. He tried running twice against Wu Jingyao (a short-distance runner with a time of 11.7 seconds), and Wu was left far behind. The key to short-distance running lies in the effectiveness of the start. Judging from Yoshioka's start, even if Liu Changchun of our country had not injured his leg, he would probably be no match for him. Kakutani Hachi and Yasushiba Haruo tried running the 1,500 meters with broad strides. Their graceful and composed demeanor was excellent. Sumiyoshi Kosaku tried throwing the javelin, tossing it lightly and sending it far beyond 140 or 150 feet. One Word: Autumn Water 112

If the law had no provisions for divorce, alimony, etc., many women would definitely think twice before experiencing the sweet kisses of men. This world could reduce a lot of tragedies. A man usually doesn't take a woman's loud scolding to heart because he knows that when a kettle of cold water is boiled through, there won't be much loud noise. Love is omnipotent and omni-evil, all depending on whether you have the confidence and the ability to control it. Love cannot be separated from carnal desire; carnal desire can be separated from love and exist independently. Love without carnal desire is like a spring flower without its fragrance. Carnal desire without love is like a weed in a barren field, cut off from nourishment. Science is omnipotent. Almost all important industrial raw materials in the world have considerable substitutes. However, scientists have never invented a substitute for women or a substitute for love. Giving cookies and candies to your dog and giving praise and admiration to your husband may destroy their habits and chastity. Modern men hope for "passionate" and "lively" girls, while old-fashioned men hope for "silent" and "shy" virgins. The two are fundamentally different, so there is a lack of chaste virgins in modern times. You can't catch fish in the river without fragrant bait, and you can't buy the hearts of women without money. However, fish sometimes cast themselves into the net without effort, and modern women are much smarter, don't even think about unconditionally surrendering their hearts.

Camel Moving House: Autumn Water 113

Houses are immovable property, as everyone knows. Because they are immovable, their completion is permanent. However, now there is a camel moving house, which is truly a rare thing in the world. This happened in the desert of North Africa, and overseas telegrams have spread the news, so it should not be groundless. I will write about it. North Africa has the Sahara Desert, which is known to all those who know geography. Although there are no lush forests, there are also natural landscapes. There are cities nearby that are operated by the French. Therefore, the Sahara is often visited by tourists. The pyramids and groups of camels are full of interest and cannot be compared to the noise of Europe. In order to revitalize the market and expand its influence, the French government has in recent years had a plan to build a large hostel in the Sahara, diverting water to form springs and transplanting trees to achieve a victory of man over nature. However, it is not easy to succeed in the wilderness. Government officials have repeatedly summoned famous architects to take on the task, but they all refused to accept the job, citing their inability to adapt to the climate. Ordinary divine laborers were also unwilling to work there for a long time. The French government had no choice but to choose a suitable place on the Mediterranean coast and build a very large hostel in preparation for moving it to the Sahara after it was built. At the end of last month, the project was completely completed. The French government then loaded the components of the hostel, such as doors, windows, wall panels, and all its internal equipment, onto the backs of camels and transported them to the Sahara. They also temporarily gathered a large number of craftsmen in the Sahara to reassemble them in the same way according to the order of transportation. It is said that each camel had to transport 200 pounds of goods at a time, rotating back and forth. It was completed in less than two weeks, and the new hostel in the Sahara will soon be completed. Then, travelers to the vast desert of northern Africa will no longer have to worry about food, clothing, and shelter. Isn't that fortunate? Autumn Water Notes: The French government's project this time cost a lot of money.

Little Knowledge: Hair, Tin, Marquis 114

After furs are exposed, they must be thoroughly cooled before being put into the box, and the box lid must be closed slowly and not slammed shut. If the heat has not dissipated and cold air enters, the fur will become damp and lose hair. Silk fabrics with linen in them are suitable for everyday wear. However, prolonged exposure to sunlight can easily cause fading, often resulting in uneven colors on the top and bottom, which is very unsightly. It is best to avoid the sun to prevent this problem. In summer, if you put a little dried Malan vegetable (a vegetable name, mostly available in the market, dried) when cooking meat, it can be stored for a long time without spoiling. When buying soy sauce for cooking, first put it in a pot and fry it slightly, then put it in a container to prevent white flowers from forming for a long time. However, once a hostel is established in the Sahara, various scientific methods will be used to overcome nature and turn useless land into a rich area, which is also very worthwhile. Moreover, the hostel built on the Mediterranean coast is well-equipped and built with the latest methods, so it is not difficult to transport it by camel.

Random Talks Before Dinner: Zheng Zhian 115

Last night, Mr. Yu Canxia invited me to drink in his "Washing Cauldron Reading Painting" studio. Many members of the Ming Society were at the table, talking about art and laughing heartily. Yao Jinqiu, a senior from Wuxing, was in high spirits and recited his couplets for the Zeng Gong Pavilion on Mozi Lake: "The sea field changes, but the small pavilion remains. We still love and admire the virtuous minister." "The mist and waves are vast, and the famous lake has been desolate since ancient times. It's useless to worry about Mo Chou." Also, the couplet for the Misty Rain Tower: "How can the Mandarin Duck River compare to the mossy river? It's like the green waves and misty scenery of our hometown, still seeing the lofty and magnificent terraces here, far surpassing the Floating Jade Pagoda." "The South Lake is not inferior to the West Lake. If a few more green mountains and beautiful scenery are added, it will be even better. Recognizing a corner of the city wall across the shore, it vaguely resembles approaching Yongjin Gate." The construction of its organization is beyond the reach of ordinary people. He also described a poem clock couplet by a Mr. Yun Jian, embedding the four characters Zhang San Li Si: "Four walls of books, a three-foot sword; half a shoulder of luggage, a Zhang Qin." It is also very wonderful. At that time, there was a thunderstorm and the oppressive heat was relieved. After a while, the rain stopped and Mr. Gong Jianhong arrived late due to the rain. He happily took his seat. Mr. Gong's poetic talent is pure and wonderful, and he was appreciated by my commander Ye Xudong, a student of Mingjing. I most love to recite his poems: "A child recites a book under the lamp, an old wife chats idly when dreams return." and "After fishing, the boat is tied to the sparse willow bank, and the mountain watcher leans against the sunset building." He also echoed the jueju of Lao Dan's Dream Record: "Joy is met in a dream, and the dream is also joyful. It is not easy to meet joy, and it is difficult to dream joy. If you dream of joy again, don't take him as a dream." It is exquisitely beautiful and worth reading. Mr. Gong highly praised Hu Yanzhu of the same society for his autumn butterfly poems in the rhyme of Yuyang's Autumn Willow: "Where is the famous flower's north lane home? The fragrant grass and the western garden guest are gradually sparse. The frost flower's life is tears in two lines, and the dew's fate is an inch of cotton." They are all excellent sentences. After the wine, I bid farewell and hurriedly recorded that Mr. Yu has a three-generation poetry manuscript. Mr. Canxia's father, Mr. Ping Han, has a legacy of Su Chi Collection, so he combined the Canxia Collection and his son Yuan Ying's Cocoon Collection and published them. I once sent his edition to Mr. Chen Shiyi of Houguan to ask for his evaluation. Houguan replied that he regretted not being able to include it in the Modern Poetry Anthology and Shiyi Studio Poetry Talks, so I also recorded this to show a glimpse of literary correspondence. Quirks: Haiyan 116

Mrs. Su, a Hui Muslim woman in Zhangjiachong outside the East Gate of Shaoyang, likes to eat salted rice. She always adds a large amount of salt to her tea and wine. When asked why, she said it was because they were bland. Also, Luo, a wealthy man in the west of the same county, likes to eat rotten food. He lets the meat breed maggots, the fruit ferment, and the tofu grow mold before eating it. He has never been sick in his life and is as healthy as a normal person.

On the ninth day, a large Buddha was newly erected outside the door, about six丈 tall, which was raised by Siamese monks.
